## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search -> read -> references -> definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls

# Fix UDP Proxy Crash on Dynamic CDS/EDS Cluster Updates

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/envoy--1ae957c1 (mirror of envoyproxy/envoy)
**Difficulty:** MEDIUM
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix

## Description

Envoy's UDP proxy filter crashes when a pre-existing cluster is updated via CDS (Cluster Discovery Service), for example when `HostSet` changes occur. The crash happens because `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `udp_proxy_filter.cc` uses `std::unordered_map::emplace()` to insert cluster info into the `cluster_infos_` map.

When a cluster with the same name already exists (i.e., it's being updated rather than added for the first time), `emplace()` silently fails — it returns the existing entry unchanged without inserting the new one. This leaves a stale `ClusterInfo` object in the map that references the old `ThreadLocalCluster`. When the old `ThreadLocalCluster` is destroyed as part of the update, the filter still holds a dangling pointer through the stale map entry, leading to a crash on the next packet.

The fix replaces `emplace()` with `insert_or_assign()` in both the per-packet-load-balancing and sticky-session code paths, so that cluster updates correctly replace the old entry.

## Task

Changes:
- 3 files modified (changelogs/current.yaml, udp_proxy_filter.cc, udp_proxy_filter_test.cc)
- 52 additions, 4 deletions

Tasks:
1. Fix `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` in `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` to use `insert_or_assign()` instead of `emplace()` in both code paths
2. Add a regression test `ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate` in the UDP proxy filter test file
3. Add a changelog entry in `changelogs/current.yaml` under `bug_fixes`

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 3 modified files updated correctly.

562026-03-11T05:45:24.866903agentmessage-
All tasks are complete. Here's a summary of the changes made:

## Summary of Changes

### 1. `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` — **Bug Fix**

**Root cause**: In `onClusterAddOrUpdate()`, `cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name, ...)` silently fails when the key already exists (standard `std::map::emplace` behavior). During a CDS/EDS cluster update, the old `ClusterInfo` (with its stale pointer to the old cluster object) remains in the map, causing a dangling pointer crash.

**Fix**: Replaced both `emplace()` calls with `insert_or_assign()`, which correctly overwrites the existing entry when the cluster name already exists. When the old `ClusterInfo` unique_ptr is replaced, its destructor runs `~ClusterInfo()` which properly cleans up all active sessions.

```cpp
// Before (buggy):
cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name, std::make_unique<PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo>(...));
cluster_infos_.emplace(cluster_name, std::make_unique<StickySessionClusterInfo>(...));

// After (fixed):
cluster_infos_.insert_or_assign(cluster_name, std::make_unique<PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo>(...));
cluster_infos_.insert_or_assign(cluster_name, std::make_unique<StickySessionClusterInfo>(...));
```

### 2. `test/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter_test.cc` — **Regression Test**

Added `TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate)` which:
1. Sets up a filter with an active session on `fake_cluster`
2. Simulates a CDS update by calling `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` with the same cluster name but a new `MockThreadLocalCluster` object
3. Verifies that old sessions are cleaned up (active count drops to 0)
4. Verifies the filter works correctly with the new cluster

### 3. `changelogs/current.yaml` — **Changelog Entry**

Added a `udp_proxy` bug fix e

map, in case the host was resolved.\n    ASSERT(host_to_sessions_[&session->host().value().get()].count(session) == 1);\n    auto host_sessions_it = host_to_sessions_.find(&session->host().value().get());\n    host_sessions_it->second.erase(session);\n    if (host_sessions_it->second.empty()) {\n      host_to_sessions_.erase(host_sessions_it);\n     const Upstream::HostConstSharedPtr& optional_host,\n                                           bool defer_socket_creation) {\n  if (!cluster_.info()\n           ->resourceManager(Upstream::ResourcePriority::Default)\n           .connections()\n           .canCreate()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot create new connection.\");\n    cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_overflow_.inc();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  if (defer_socket_creation) {\n    ASSERT(!optional_host);\n    return chooseHost(addresses.peer_, nullptr);\n  if (host == nullptr) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot find any valid host.\");\n    cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_none_healthy_.inc();\n                 HeterogeneousActiveSessionEqual(false))) {}\n\nNetwork::FilterStatus UdpProxyFilter::StickySessionClusterInfo::onData(Network::UdpRecvData& data) {\n  bool defer_socket = filter_.config_->hasSessionFilters() || filter_.config_->tunnelingConfig();\n  const auto active_session_it = sessions_.find(data.addresses_);\n  ActiveSession* active_session;\n  if (active_session_it == sessions_.end()) {\n    active_session = createSession(std::move(data.addresses_), nullptr, defer_socket);\n    if (active_session == nullptr) {\n      return Network::FilterStatus::StopIteration;\n    }\n  } else {\n    active_session = active_session_it->get();\n    // We defer the socket creation when the session includes filters, so the filters can be\n    // iterated before choosing the host, to allow dynamically choosing upstream host. Due to this,\n    // we can't perform health checks during a session.\n    // TODO(ohadvano): add similar functionality that is performed after session filter chain\n    // iteration to signal filters about the unhealthy host, or replace the host during the session.\n    if (!defer_socket &&\n        active_session->host().value().get().coarseHealth() == Upstream::Host::Health::Unhealthy) {\n      // If a host becomes unhealthy, we optimally would like to replace it with a new session\n      // to a healthy host. We may eventually want to make this behavior configurable, but for now\n      // this will be the universal behavior.\n      auto host = chooseHost(data.addresses_.peer_, nullptr);\n      if (host != nullptr && host->coarseHealth() != Upstream::Host::Health::Unhealthy &&\n          host.get() != &active_session->host().value().get()) {\n        ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"upstream session unhealthy, recreating the session\");\n        removeSession(active_session);\n        active_session = createSession(std::move(data.addresses_), host, false);\n      } else {\n        // In this case we could not get a better host, so just keep using the current session.\n        ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"upstream session unhealthy, but unable to get a better host\");\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  active_session->onData(data);\n\n  return Network::FilterStatus::StopIteration;\n}\n\nUdpProxyFilter::PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo::PerPacketLoadBalancingClusterInfo(\n    UdpProxyFilter& filter, UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::onIdleTimer() {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"session idle timeout: downstream={} local={}\", addresses_.peer_->asStringView(),\n            addresses_.local_->asStringView());\n  cluster_.filter_.config_->stats().idle_timeout_.inc();\n  cluster_.removeSession(this);\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::onReadReady() {\n  resetIdleTimer();\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): We should not be passing *addresses_.local_ to this function as we are\n  //                     not trying to populate the local address for received packets.\n  uint32_t packets_dropped = 0;\n  const Api::IoErrorPtr result = Network::Utility::readPacketsFromSocket(\n      udp_socket_->ioHandle(), *addresses_.local_, *this, cluster_.filter_.config_->timeSource(),\n      cluster_.filter_.config_->upstreamSocketConfig().prefer_gro_, /*allow_mmsg=*/true,\n      packets_dropped);\n  if (result == nullptr) {\n    udp_socket_->ioHandle().activateFileEvents(Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n    return;\n  }\n  if (result->getErrorCode() != Api::IoError::IoErrorCode::Again) {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_rx_errors_.inc();\n  }\n  // Flush out buffered data at the end of IO event.\n  cluster_.filter_.read_callbacks_->udpListener().flush();\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onNewSession() {\n  if (cluster_.filter_.config_->accessLogFlushInterval().has_value() &&\n      !cluster_.filter_.config_->sessionAccessLogs().empty()) {\n    access_log_flush_timer_ =\n        cluster_.filter_.read_callbacks_->udpListener().dispatcher().createTimer(\n            [this] { onAccessLogFlushInterval(); });\n    rearmAccessLogFlushTimer();\n  }\n\n  // Set UUID for the session. This is used for logging and tracing.\n  udp_session_info_.setStreamIdProvider(std::make_shared<StreamInfo::StreamIdProviderImpl>(\n      cluster_.filter_.config_->randomGenerator().uuid()));\n\n  for (auto& active_read_filter : read_filters_) {\n    if (active_read_filter->initialized_) {\n      // The filter may call continueFilterChain() in onNewSession(), causing next\n      // filters to iterate onNewSession(), so check that it was not called before.\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    active_read_filter->initialized_ = true;\n    auto status = active_read_filter->read_filter_->onNewSession();\n    if (status == ReadFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return createUpstream();\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onData(Network::UdpRecvData& data) {\n  ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"received {} byte datagram from downstream: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            data.buffer_->length(), addresses_.peer_->asStringView(),\n            addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host_ != nullptr ? host_->address()->asStringView() : \"unknown\");\n\n  const uint64_t rx_buffer_length = data.buffer_->length();\n  cluster_.filter_.config_->stats().downstream_sess_rx_bytes_.add(rx_buffer_length);\n  session_stats_.downstream_sess_rx_bytes_ += rx_buffer_length;\n  cluster_.filter_.config_->stats().downstream_sess_rx_datagrams_.inc();\n  ++session_stats_.downstream_sess_rx_datagrams_;\n  resetIdleTimer();\n\n  for (auto& active_read_filter : read_filters_) {\n    auto status = active_read_filter->read_filter_->onData(data);\n    if (status == ReadFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n\n  writeUpstream(data);\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::writeUpstream(Network::UdpRecvData& data) {\n  if (!udp_socket_) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot write upstream because the socket was not created.\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // NOTE: On the first write, a local ephemeral port is bound, and thus this write can fail due to\n  //       port exhaustion. To avoid exhaustion, UDP sockets will be connected and associated with\n  //       a 4-tuple including the local IP, and the UDP port may be reused for multiple\n  //       connections unless use_original_src_ip_ is set. When use_original_src_ip_ is set, the\n  //       socket should not be connected since the source IP will be changed.\n  // NOTE: We do not specify the local IP to use for the sendmsg call if use_original_src_ip_ is not\n  //       set. We allow the OS to select the right IP based on outbound routing rules if\n  //       use_original_src_ip_ is not set, else use downstream peer IP as local IP.\n  if (!connected_ && !use_original_src_ip_) {\n    Api::SysCallIntResult rc = udp_socket_->ioHandle().connect(host_->address());\n    if (SOCKET_FAILURE(rc.return_value_)) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot connect: ({}) {}\", rc.errno_, errorDetails(rc.errno_));\n      cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_errors_.inc();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    connected_ = true;\n  }\n\n  ASSERT((connected_ || use_original_src_ip_) && udp_socket_ && host_);\n\n  const uint64_t tx_buffer_length = data.buffer_->length();\n  ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"writing {} byte datagram upstream: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            tx_buffer_length, addresses_.peer_->asStringView(), addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host_->address()->asStringView());\n\n  const Network::Address::Ip* local_ip = use_original_src_ip_ ? addresses_.peer_->ip() : nullptr;\n  Api::IoCallUint64Result rc = Network::Utility::writeToSocket(\n      udp_socket_->ioHandle(), *data.buffer_, local_ip, *host_->address());\n\n  if (!rc.ok()) {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_errors_.inc();\n  } else {\n    cluster_.cluster_stats_.sess_tx_datagrams_.inc();\n    cluster_.cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_tx_bytes_total_.add(tx_buffer_length);\n  }\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onContinueFilterChain(ActiveReadFilter* filter) {\n  ASSERT(filter != nullptr);\n\n  std::list<ActiveReadFilterPtr>::iterator entry = std::next(filter->entry());\n  for (; entry != read_filters_.end(); entry++) {\n    if (!(*entry)->read_filter_ || (*entry)->initialized_) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    (*entry)->initialized_ = true;\n    auto status = (*entry)->read_filter_->onNewSession();\n    if (status == ReadFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (!createUpstream()) {\n    cluster_.removeSession(this);\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::createUpstream() {\n  if (udp_socket_) {\n    // A session filter may call on continueFilterChain(), after already creating the socket,\n    // so we first check that the socket was not created already.\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  if (!host_) {\n    host_ = cluster_.chooseHost(addresses_.peer_, &udp_session_info_);\n    if (host_ == nullptr) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cannot find any valid host.\");\n      cluster_.cluster_.info()->trafficStats()->upstream_cx_none_healthy_.inc();\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  udp_session_info_.upstreamInfo()->setUpstreamHost(host_);\n  cluster_.addSession(host_.get(), this);\n  createUdpSocket(host_);\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::createUdpSocket(const Upstream::HostConstSharedPtr& host) {\n  // NOTE: The socket call can only fail due to memory/fd exhaustion. No local ephemeral port\n  //       is bound until the first packet is sent to the upstream host.\n  udp_socket_ = cluster_.filter_.createUdpSocket(host);\n  udp_socket_->ioHandle().initializeFileEvent(\n      cluster_.filter_.read_callbacks_->udpListener().dispatcher(),\n      [this](uint32_t) { onReadReady(); }, Event::PlatformDefaultTriggerType,\n      Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"creating new session: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            addresses_.peer_->asStringView(), addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host->address()->asStringView());\n\n  if (use_original_src_ip_) {\n    const Network::Socket::OptionsSharedPtr socket_options =\n        Network::SocketOptionFactory::buildIpTransparentOptions();\n    const bool ok = Network::Socket::applyOptions(\n        socket_options, *udp_socket_, envoy::config::core::v3::SocketOption::STATE_PREBIND);\n\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(ok, \"Should never occur!\");\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"The original src is enabled for address {}.\",\n              addresses_.peer_->asStringView());\n  }\n\n  // TODO(mattklein123): Enable dropped packets socket option. In general the Socket abstraction\n  // does not work well right now for client sockets. It's too heavy weight and is aimed at listener\n  // sockets. We need to figure out how to either refactor Socket into something that works better\n  // for this use case or allow the socket option abstractions to work directly against an IO\n  // handle.\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::onInjectReadDatagramToFilterChain(ActiveReadFilter* filter,\n                                                                      Network::UdpRecvData& data) {\n  ASSERT(filter != nullptr);\n\n  std::list<ActiveReadFilterPtr>::iterator entry = std::next(filter->entry());\n  for (; entry != read_filters_.end(); entry++) {\n    if (!(*entry)->read_filter_) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    auto status = (*entry)->read_filter_->onData(data);\n    if (status == ReadFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n\n }\n\n  writeDownstream(data);\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::UdpActiveSession::processPacket(\n    Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr local_address,\n    Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr idle_timer_->enableTimer(cluster_.filter_.config_->sessionTimeout());\n}\n\nvoid UdpProxyFilter::ActiveSession::processUpstreamDatagram(Network::UdpRecvData& recv_data) {\n  for (auto& active_write_filter : write_filters_) {\n    auto status = active_write_filter->write_filter_->onWrite(recv_data);\n    if (status == WriteFilterStatus::StopIteration) {\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n\n ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"writing {} byte datagram downstream: downstream={} local={} upstream={}\",\n            tx_buffer_length, addresses_.peer_->asStringView(), addresses_.local_->asStringView(),\n            host_ != nullptr ? host_->address()->asStringView() : \"unknown\");\n\n  Network::UdpSendData data{addresses_.local_->ip(), *addresses_.peer_, *recv_data.buffer_};\n  const EXPECT_EQ(self_ip->addressAsString(), local_ip->addressAsString());\n                  }\n                  // For suppression of clang-tidy NewDeleteLeaks rule, don't use the ternary\n                  // operator.\n                  if (sys_errno == 0) {\n                    return makeNoError(data.size());\n                  } else {\n                    return makeError(sys_errno);\n                  }\n                }));\n      }\n    }\n\n    void recvDataFromUpstream(const std::string& data, int recv_sys_errno = 0,\n                              int send_sys_errno = 0) {\n      EXPECT_CALL(*idle_timer_, enableTimer(parent_.config_->sessionTimeout(), nullptr));\n\n      if (parent_.expect_gro_) {\n        EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, supportsUdpGro());\n      }\n      EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, supportsMmsg()).Times(1u);\n      // Return the datagram.\n      EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, recvmsg(_, 1, _, _))\n          .WillOnce(\n              Invoke([this, data, recv_sys_errno](\n                         Buffer::RawSlice* slices, const uint64_t, uint32_t,\n                         Network::IoHandle::RecvMsgOutput& output) -> Api::IoCallUint64Result {\n                if (recv_sys_errno != 0) {\n                  return makeError(recv_sys_errno);\n                } else {\n                  ASSERT(data.size() <= slices[0].len_);\n                  memcpy(slices[0].mem_, data.data(), data.size());\n                  output.msg_[0].peer_address_ = upstream_address_;\n                  return makeNoError(data.size());\n                }\n              }));\n      if (recv_sys_errno == 0) {\n        // Send the datagram downstream.\n        EXPECT_CALL(parent_.callbacks_.udp_listener_, send(_))\n            .WillOnce(Invoke([data, send_sys_errno](\n                                 const Network::UdpSendData& send_data) -> Api::IoCallUint64Result {\n              // TODO(mattklein123): Verify peer/local address.\n              EXPECT_EQ(send_data.buffer_.toString(), data);\n              if (send_sys_errno == 0) {\n                send_data.buffer_.drain(send_data.buffer_.length());\n                return makeNoError(data.size());\n              } else {\n                return makeError(send_sys_errno);\n              }\n            }));\n        // Return an EAGAIN result.\n        EXPECT_CALL(*socket_->io_handle_, recvmsg(_, 1, _, _))\n            .WillOnce(Return(ByMove(\n                Api::IoCallUint64Result(0, Network::IoSocketError::getIoSocketEagainError()))));\n      }\n\n      // Kick off the receive.\n      file_event_cb_(Event::FileReadyType::Read);\n    }\n\n    UdpProxyFilterTest& parent_;\n    const Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr upstream_address_;\n    Event::MockTimer* idle_timer_{};\n    NiceMock<Network::MockSocket>* socket_;\n    std::map<int, std::map<int, int>> sock_opts_;\n    Event::FileReadyCb file_event_cb_;\n  };\n\n  UdpProxyFilterTest()\n      : UdpProxyFilterTest(Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(peer_ip_address_)) {}\n\n  explicit UdpProxyFilterTest(Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr&& peer_address)\n      : os_calls_(&os_sys_calls_),\n        upstream_address_(Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(upstream_ip_address_)),\n        peer_address_(std::move(peer_address)) {\n    // Disable strict mock warnings.\n    ON_CALL(*factory_context_.server_factory_context_.access_log_manager_.file_, write(_))\n        .WillByDefault(\n            Invoke([&](absl::string_view data) { output_.push_back(std::string(data)); }));\n    ON_CALL(os_sys_calls_, supportsIpTransparent(_)).WillByDefault(Return(true));\n    EXPECT_CALL(os_sys_calls_, supportsUdpGro()).Times(AtLeast(0)).WillRepeatedly(Return(true));\n    EXPECT_CALL(callbacks_, udpListener()).Times(AtLeast(0));\n    EXPECT_CALL(\n        *factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_.lb_.host_,\n        address())\n        .WillRepeatedly(Return(upstream_address_));\n    EXPECT_CALL(\n        *factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_.thread_local_cluster_.lb_.host_,\n        coarseHealth())\n        .WillRepeatedly(Return(Upstream::Host::Health::Healthy));\n  }\n\n  ~UdpProxyFilterTest() override { EXPECT_CALL(callbacks_.udp_listener_, onDestroy()); }\n\n  void setup(const envoy::extensions::filters::udp::udp_proxy::v3::UdpProxyConfig& config,\n             bool has_cluster = true, bool expect_gro = true) {\n    config_ = std::make_shared<UdpProxyFilterConfigImpl>(factory_context_, config);\n    EXPECT_CALL(factory_context_.server_factory_context_.cluster_manager_,\n buffer) {\n    Network::UdpRecvData data;\n    data.addresses_.peer_ = Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(peer_address);\n    data.addresses_.local_ = Network::Utility::parseInternetAddressAndPort(local_address);\n    data.buffer_ = std::make_unique<Buffer::OwnedImpl>(buffer);\n    data.receive_time_ = MonotonicTime(std::chrono::seconds(0));\n    filter_->onData(data);\n  }\n\n  void expectSessionCreate(const Network::Address::InstanceConstSharedPtr& address) {\n    test_sessions_.emplace_back(*this, address);\n    TestSession& new_session = .WillOnce(Return(ByMove(Network::SocketPtr{test_sessions_.back().socket_})));\n    EXPECT_CALL(\n        *new_session.socket_->io_handle_,\n        createFileEvent_(_, _,        .cluster_.info_->traffic_stats_->upstream_cx_tx_bytes_total_.value());\n\n  test_sessions_[0].recvDataFromUpstream(\"world2\", 0, SOCKET_ERROR_MSG_SIZE);\n  checkTransferStats(5 /*rx_bytes*/, 1 EXPECT_THAT(output_.front(), testing::HasSubstr(\"session_complete\"));\n}\n\nclass HttpUpstreamImplTest : public testing::Test {\npublic:\n  struct HeaderToAdd {\n    std::string key_;\n    std::string value_;\n  };\n\n  Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl\n  expectedHeaders(bool is_ssl = false, bool use_post = false,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_authority = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<std::string> opt_path = absl::nullopt,\n                  absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    // In case connect-udp is used, Envoy expect the H2 headers to be normalized with H1,\n    // so expect that the request headers here match H1 headers, even though\n    // eventually H2 headers will be sent. When the headers are normalized to H1, the method\n    // is replaced with GET, a header with the 'upgrade' key is added with 'connect-udp'\n    // value and a header with the 'connection' key is added with 'Upgrade' value.\n    std::string scheme = is_ssl ? \"https\" : \"http\";\n    std::string authority =\n        opt_authority.has_value() ? opt_authority.value() : \"default.host.com:10\";\n    std::string method = use_post ? \"POST\" : \"GET\";\n    std::string path =\n        opt_path.has_value() ? opt_path.value() : \"/.well-known/masque/udp/default.target.host/20/\";\n\n    auto headers = Http::TestRequestHeaderMapImpl{\n        {\":scheme\", scheme}, {\":authority\", authority}, {\":method\", method}, {\":path\", path}};\n\n    if (!use_post) {\n      headers.addCopy(\"capsule-protocol\", \"?1\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"upgrade\", \"connect-udp\");\n      headers.addCopy(\"connection\", \"Upgrade\");\n    }\n\n    if (header_to_add) {\n      headers.addCopy(header_to_add.value().key_, header_to_add.value().value_);\n    }\n\n    return headers;\n  }\n\n  void Http::Status {\n          EXPECT_THAT(&headers, HeaderMapEqualIgnoreOrder(&expected_headers));\n          EXPECT_FALSE(end_stream);\n          return absl::OkStatus();\n        }));\n\n stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.proxy_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(proxy_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n\n    if (target_port) {\n      stream_info_.filterState()->setData(\n          \"udp.connect.target_port\",\n          std::make_shared<StreamInfo::UInt32AccessorImpl>(target_port.value()),\n          Envoy::StreamInfo::FilterState::StateType::Mutable);\n    }\n  }\n\n  void setup(absl::optional<HeaderToAdd> header_to_add = absl::nullopt) {\n    Protobuf::RepeatedPtrField<envoy::config::core::v3::HeaderValueOption> headers_to_add;\n    if (header_to_add) {\n {
  "message": "All tasks are complete. Here's a summary of all changes made to fix the UDP proxy crash on dynamic CDS/EDS cluster updates:\n\n## Changes Made\n\n### 1. `source/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter.cc` \u2014 Bug Fix\n**Lines 52 & 55**: Replaced `cluster_infos_.emplace(...)` with `cluster_infos_.insert_or_assign(...)` in both branches of `onClusterAddOrUpdate()`:\n\n- **Per-packet load balancing branch** (line 52): `emplace` \u2192 `insert_or_assign`\n- **Sticky session branch** (line 55): `emplace` \u2192 `insert_or_assign`\n\n**Root cause**: `std::map::emplace()` silently fails when the key already exists. During a CDS/EDS cluster update, `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` is called with the same cluster name but a new cluster object. With `emplace`, the old `ClusterInfo` (containing a dangling pointer to the destroyed old cluster) remained in the map, causing a crash. With `insert_or_assign`, the old entry is replaced, its destructor runs, and all stale sessions are properly cleaned up.\n\n### 2. `test/extensions/filters/udp/udp_proxy/udp_proxy_filter_test.cc` \u2014 Regression Test\nAdded `TEST_F(UdpProxyFilterTest, ClusterDynamicInfoMapUpdate)` at line 830 (between `ClusterDynamicAddAndRemoval` and `MaxSessionsCircuitBreaker`). The test:\n1. Sets up a filter with an active session on `fake_cluster`\n2. Simulates a CDS update by calling `onClusterAddOrUpdate()` with the same cluster name but a new `NiceMock<Upstream::MockThreadLocalCluster>` object\n3. Verifies old sessions are cleaned up (active count drops from 1 to 0)\n4. Verifies the filter works correctly with the new cluster (new session can be created)\n\nAlso corrected the `NoUpstreamClusterAtCreation` test to match the original simple form (using `accessLogConfig` with `no_route` metric).\n\n### 3. `changelogs/current.yaml` \u2014 Changelog Entry\nAdded a `udp_proxy` bug fix entry in the `bug_fixes` section documenting the crash fix with `emplace` \u2192 `insert_or_assign`."
